## 🌱 Seed Data Source of Truth

> **Seed data truth**: The SeedPanel documentation built in SP1/P10 — including each collection's `slugPattern`, `mediaFields`, PII field list, and the searchable/filterable/sortable column metadata table — is the **canonical reference** for all 23 collections. Seed files in `appkit/src/seed/` are updated **as we go** (same session as any schema change — never defer seed updates to a later session). The P23–P31 scale sessions expand *counts* only; the field shapes and metadata are already correct per SP1.

---

## ⛔ Non-Negotiable Rules (apply to every task, every commit)

| Rule | Detail |
|------|--------|
| **🛑 STOP AND ASK — never auto-decide** | Before choosing an approach, skipping any part of a spec, marking something ✅, deviating from the tracker description, or deciding something is "over-engineering" — **STOP. Write out what you're about to do and WHY. Ask the user to confirm before proceeding.** Many past regressions were caused by silent autonomous decisions. The user may be fixing those regressions in a parallel session right now. If you are uncertain about ANY part of a task, ask. The cost of one question is near zero; the cost of a wrong decision compounds across every future session. |
| **⚠️ Some ✅ tasks may have regressions** | The user has confirmed that tasks marked ✅ in this tracker are not all working correctly in the browser. If you touch a ✅ area, re-verify it works before assuming it is fine. If you discover a ✅ task is broken, change its status to ⚠️ done-but-verify and add a note — do NOT silently skip it. |
| **🔍 Never fix without verifying it is actually broken** | Before touching any code in response to a bug report or plan note: (1) **Read the current source file** — do not rely on bug descriptions from memory, plans, or old session notes. (2) **Confirm the bug is present** — if the code already handles the case correctly, mark the bug as resolved and move on. (3) **Check when the file was last modified** — `git log -1 -- <file>` tells you if it was already fixed in a recent session. A bug documented in a plan file or memory may already be fixed. Acting on a stale bug report causes unnecessary churn and can introduce regressions where none existed. |
| **✅ means fully done per THIS tracker** | A small code fix does NOT equal task complete. ✅ means the FULL description in the tracker is implemented, TypeScript passes, and it works in the browser. If a file was modified to partially fix something but the tracker's full spec is unmet, the task stays ⏳. When in doubt, re-read the tracker definition and verify in the browser before marking ✅. |
| **Never silently skip or defer a spec component** | If any bullet point or sub-task in a task's spec column is not being done, you MUST either: (a) do it now, or (b) create a new explicit ⏳ task for it with a reference like "deferred from J7: xyz" — then note the new task ID in the parent's done notes. A "deferred — over-engineering" comment alone is NOT acceptable. Marking ✅ while parts of the spec are unbuilt is the most harmful mistake in this tracker. Every session that comes after inherits the assumption that ✅ means complete. |
| **No stale "remaining: P5 seed data" style notes on ✅ tasks** | If a ✅ note references a pending/superseded task as a blocker ("remaining: P5 seed data"), immediately verify whether the blocker has since been resolved and update the note. Stale ✅ notes are silent lies — they make future sessions skip re-verification. |
| **UI never crashes** | Missing data, renamed fields, absent API keys → empty state / graceful fallback. Never a white screen or thrown error. Schema breaks are OK (TS catches them); runtime UI breaks are not. |
| **Props always have defaults** | Every new component prop that is optional must have a fallback value. Components must render with minimal data. |
| **No half-renames** | Renaming a field, route, or prop = one atomic commit covering both producer and consumer. Never leave both old and new names live at once. |
| **Reuse before creating** | Search appkit before writing a new component. Primitives → `appkit/src/ui/`. Feature components → `appkit/src/features/[domain]/`. Pages are thin wrappers only. |
| **Navigation never regresses** | Public navbar, mobile bottom bar, admin/store/user sidebars, breadcrumbs must always render correctly. Route changes require updating all link references atomically. |
| **Search + slug system preserved** | Query params (`q=`, `f=`, `s=`, `p=`, `ps=`, `cursor=`) must keep working. Slug prefixes are fixed (see Tier 0-pre). All new resource types must register their prefix. |
| **Sticky toolbars stay sticky** | Filter bars, bulk action bars, sort controls on listing pages must remain visible and functional on scroll. Never change their layout without visual verification. |
| **0 TS errors before commit** | `npx tsc --noEmit` must pass in both `letitrip.in/` and `appkit/`. Both repos committed together when both change. |
| **No hardcoded colors** | Never use `#hex`, `rgb()`, or `rgba()` in component CSS files or inline `style={}` props. All colors must come from `var(--appkit-color-*)` CSS custom properties or Tailwind semantic tokens. Only token definition files (`globals.css`, `tokens.css`) and SVG assets are exempt. Social brand colors get their own `--appkit-color-instagram` etc. tokens. |
| **No hardcoded layout values** | Never use raw pixel values for breakpoints (`@media (min-width: 768px)`), z-index integers, spacing/height/width, font sizes, border-radius, or box-shadows in component CSS files or inline `style={}` props. Use `@screen md { }`, `var(--appkit-z-modal)`, `var(--appkit-size-input-md)`, `var(--appkit-shadow-md)`, `var(--appkit-font-size-2xs)` etc. Token definition files and `tailwind.config.ts` are the only exceptions. Tailwind arbitrary syntax `p-[44px]`, `z-[50]`, `text-[10px]` is also banned — use a named token class. |
| **Quality over speed — think deeply, session-split when needed** | Every task deserves full attention. Do NOT rush to mark tasks done. Before implementing, re-read the relevant source files and understand the full impact. If context starts to feel fuzzy (too many files in mind, losing track of what changed), stop and start a new chat session — do NOT push forward with degraded context. A good rule of thumb: no more than 10–20 tasks per session before resetting. Better to pause, summarise, and continue fresh than to produce low-quality or incorrect output. |
| **Buttons are actions; links are navigation — never mix** | `<Button>` (appkit) triggers a mutation, opens a modal, or submits a form — it NEVER navigates. Never use `<Button onClick={() => router.push(...)}>`. For navigation use `<Link href={ROUTES.*}>` (Next.js) or `<TextLink href={ROUTES.*}>` (appkit). For styled-button navigation use the `asChild` pattern with `<Link>` inside. Every `href` must reference a `ROUTES.*` constant — no hardcoded strings like `href="/products"`. |

---

## 🔁 Recurrent Root Cause Patterns

> These patterns have caused multiple bugs across many sessions. Check against this list before touching any related area. Bug IDs reference the first known instance.

| # | Pattern | Watch for |
|---|---------|-----------|
| 1 | **Firestore field absence ≠ false** | `where("isAuction","==",false)` returns 0 when field is absent. Every seed doc MUST have all filtered boolean fields explicitly set. (J13) |
| 2 | **Missing Firestore composite indexes** | Multi-`where` + `orderBy` queries throw `FAILED_PRECONDITION` silently in prod. Add to `appkit/firebase/base/firestore.indexes.json`; never edit the root file directly. (J13) |
| 3 | **Tailwind class purging** | Classes only inside appkit are purged in prod unless safelisted in `tailwind.config.js` or pre-compiled into `dist/tailwind-utilities.css`. (HF87-1) |
| 4 | **SSR shape mismatches** | Repository methods return `FirebaseSieveResult`; views expect domain shapes (e.g. `{ posts: [] }`). Always transform before passing as `initialData`. (J14) |
| 5 | **Component prop API drift** | appkit props evolve (`open` → `isOpen`, `showToast(obj)` → `showToast(msg, variant)`). Always read the component source — never assume API from memory. (HF86-4) |
| 6 | **Vercel Lambda dynamic require** | `(module as any).require(...)` bypasses Vercel's output file tracer. Force-include with `experimental.outputFileTracingIncludes`. (HF87-2) |
| 7 | **Dual `@types/react` instances** | appkit pinning `@types/react` creates dual instances with root. Use `peerDependencies` + `overrides`. (HF89-ts) |
| 8 | **Slot-shell render props not passed** | Calling any appkit view shell with zero render props = layout skeleton with no content. Always wire all `renderXxx` props. |
| 9 | **`createWithId` bypasses BaseRepository hooks** | PII encryption / validation overrides are skipped. Always override `createWithId` in the subclass too. (HF86-3) |
| 10 | **CSS @import of node_modules in globals.css** | Turbopack inlines `@import` before PostCSS — breaks tailwindcss. Import via JS in `layout.tsx` instead. (CSS-import) |
| 11 | **Stale bug/plan descriptions** | Plan files and memory entries describe what was true when written, not now. Always verify the bug still exists by reading the current source file before writing any fix. (Rule #4) |

---

## 🗺️ Session Roadmap *(read this at the start of every session)*

### Session Start Checklist

```
1. Find the next ⬜ session row below → read ALL task notes for that session in the tier tables
2. Re-read every source file you'll touch — never code from memory
3. Run: npx tsc --noEmit (letitrip.in/ AND appkit/) → must show 0 errors BEFORE you begin
4. After each task: tsc → 0 errors → commit atomically → mark ✅ in the tier table above
5. If > 15 tasks done OR context feels fuzzy → STOP → update tracker → start fresh session
Rules to keep top-of-mind every task:
  · No #hex / rgb() in CSS or inline style={} — use var(--appkit-color-*)
  · No raw px breakpoints, z-index ints, or box-shadows — use var(--appkit-z-*) / @screen md
  · <Button> = action only; <Link href={ROUTES.*}> = navigation; never onClick={() => router.push()}
  · No half-renames; no silent failures; no hardcoded route strings
  · UI never crashes — every component renders with missing/null data (empty state, not white screen)
  · Before fixing a bug: READ the current source file first — it may already be fixed (Rule #4)
  · Before any schema change: check Recurrent Root Cause Patterns table above — especially #1 (Firestore boolean fields) and #2 (composite indexes)
```

### Dependency chains that control ordering

| Chain | Must-do order |
|-------|--------------|
| TypeScript | X1 first; 0 errors before every commit |
| Seed data | P11 → P12–P15 → P16–P19 → P21–P22 → P20 → P10 → P23–P26 → P27–P29 → P30 → P31 |
| Infra components | H1 + I4 + I8 + I5 before any CRUD forms that need them |
| Homepage sections | HS1 → HS2 + HS3 → HS4 + HS5 |
| Site settings → CDN | VA8 (settings UI) before I7 (watermark proxy reads settings) |
| Admin before Store | A1 patterns → C1 + C2 (store products inherit admin form patterns) |
| SC chain | SC1 → SC2 + SC3 → SC4 |
| SR chain | SR1 → SR2 + SR3 |
| RC chain | RC2 (extend ROUTES) → RC1 (centralise nav) → RC3 (audit violations) |
| GP chain | GP1 → GP2 |
| Color tokens | X7a → X7b |
| Layout tokens | X8a → X8b |
| SB chain | SB1-A–G → SB1-H–L → SB2 → SB3 → SB4 → SB5–SB10 → SB11 (SB11 needs SB1-A listingType + SB4 PrizeDraw + SB9 raffle schemas) |
| RBAC chain | RBAC1 → RBAC2 + RBAC10 → RBAC3 + RBAC7 → RBAC4 + RBAC5 → RBAC6 + RBAC8 + RBAC9 |
| BAN chain | BAN1 → BAN2 → BAN3 → BAN4 → BAN5 + BAN6 → BAN7 + BAN8 + BAN9 |
| GD chain | GD1–GD11 (independent); GD12 depends on RBAC8; GD13–GD22 (independent) |

### Slug prefix table (enforced everywhere):

| Resource | Prefix | Example |
|----------|--------|---------|
| Product | `product-` | `product-hot-wheels-redline-vintage` |
| Auction | `auction-` | `auction-pokemon-charizard-1st-edition` |
| Pre-order | `preorder-` | `preorder-dbz-goku-ultra-ego` |
| Store | `store-` | `store-mistys-water-cards` |
| Category | `category-` | `category-action-figures` |
| Brand | `brand-` | `brand-hot-wheels` |
| Event | `event-` | `event-summer-holo-sale-2026` |
| Blog post | `blog-` | `blog-how-to-grade-pokemon-cards` |
| Review | `review-` | `review-[productSlug]-[userId-short]` |
| User profile | `user-` | `user-mohsin-c` |
| FAQ | `faq-` | `faq-how-does-bidding-work` |
| Coupon | `coupon-` | `coupon-summer20` |
| Section | `section-` | `section-hot-wheels-franchise` |
| Nav item | `nav-` | `nav-new-arrivals` |
| Sub-listing category | `sublisting-` | `sublisting-base-set-charizard-108-120` |

Code is correct. Seed data (P17) must use matching auction slugs as productId in bids. |
| J11 | Product detail: seller section links to store page, not user profile | S | ✅ | Session 67 | **Re-fixed 2026-05-07**: Session 60 audit was wrong — seed data uses `storeId` (not `storeSlug`), so detail views were falling back to `ROUTES.PUBLIC.SELLER_DETAIL(sellerId)` (user profile), not the store page. Fix: (1) All three detail views (`AuctionDetailPageView`, `ProductDetailPageView`, `PreOrderDetailPageView`) now read `storeId` as fallback when `storeSlug` is absent — `storeHref` now correctly resolves to `ROUTES.PUBLIC.STORE_DETAIL`. | J13 | Products listing (standard) shows "No products found" — auctions/pre-orders unaffected | M | ✅ | Session 76-infra (2026-05-10) | **Two compounding root causes:** (1) All 20 standard product seed docs had no `isAuction` or `isPreOrder` fields — Firestore `where("isAuction", "==", false)` returns 0 docs when the field is absent (undefined ≠ false). Fixed: added `isAuction: false, isPreOrder: false` to all 20 entries in `appkit/src/seed/products-standard-seed-data.ts`. (2) Missing Firestore composite index `(status ASC, isAuction ASC, createdAt DESC)` — query throws FAILED_PRECONDITION, silently caught as null initialData, staleTime:Infinity prevents client refetch. Fixed: added both `(status, isAuction, createdAt)` and `(status, isAuction, isPreOrder, createdAt)` composite indexes to `appkit/firebase/base/firestore.indexes.json` (the permanent source that `firebase-merge.mjs` reads) and to the merged `firestore.indexes.json`. **Re-seed products collection after deploying indexes.** |
| J14 | Blog listing page shows no posts (initialData shape mismatch) | S | ✅ | Session 76-infra (2026-05-10) | `BlogIndexPageView` SSR fetched via `blogRepository.listPublished()` which returns `FirebaseSieveResult` `{ items, total, page, pageSize, totalPages, hasMore }`. But `initialData` was passed directly to `BlogIndexListing` which calls `useBlogPosts` expecting `BlogListResponse` `{ posts, meta }`. `posts` field was always undefined → empty array → `staleTime:Infinity` (since initialData !== undefined) → client never refetched. Fixed in `appkit/src/features/blog/components/BlogIndexPageView.tsx`: transform SSR result to `BlogListResponse` shape before passing. If SSR fails → `undefined` initialData → staleTime=0 → client fetches. |
| J15 | Events listing page shows no events — wrong default status filter | S | ✅ | Session 76-infra (2026-05-10) | `EventsListPageView.buildEventFilters()` defaulted to `parts.push("status==published")` but events have no "published" status — valid statuses are DRAFT/ACTIVE/PAUSED/ENDED. SSR returned valid-but-empty result → initialData set → staleTime:Infinity → client never refetched. Fixed in `appkit/src/features/events/components/EventsListPageView.tsx` line 24: changed default from `"status==published"` to `"status==active"`. |
| J16 | Blog related post cards not clickable | S | ✅ | Session 89 (2026-05-11) | `BlogCard` wraps in `<Link>` only when `href` prop is provided. `renderRelatedCard` in `BlogPostPageClient.tsx` passed `<BlogCard post={relatedPost} />` with no `href` → static non-navigable card. Fixed: (1) `BlogPostPageClient.tsx` now imports `ROUTES` and passes `href={\`/${locale}${String(ROUTES.BLOG.ARTICLE(relatedPost.slug))}\`}`. (2) `BlogPostView.tsx` fallback `BlogCard` (rendered when no `renderRelatedCard` prop) also lacked `href` — fixed to pass `String(ROUTES.BLOG.ARTICLE(rel.slug))`. Both fixes committed. |
| J17 | Event participate button shows "something went wrong" for logged-in users | S | ✅ | Session 89 (2026-05-11) | `POST /api/events/[id]/entries` used `createRouteHandler` with no `auth` or `authOptional` option → session cookie never read → `user` always `undefined` → `enterEvent()` saw no user → threw auth error even for authenticated users. Fixed: (1) Added `authOptional?: boolean` to `RouteHandlerOptions` in `appkit/src/next/api/routeHandler.ts` — reads session if cookie present, continues as anonymous on failure. (2) Added `displayName?: string` to `RouteUser` interface. (3) Route now uses `authOptional: true`. `enterEvent` already handles both user-present and anonymous cases correctly. |

## Tier UX — Form Shell & Edit Experience *(build in Session 77-ux, use from Session 77 onward)*

> **Core principle**: Never navigate to a new page for a form. Every create/edit uses a shell overlay that keeps the user in context. Three shells cover all cases: FormShell (full-width, complex), QuickFormDrawer (narrow, ≤ 6 fields), InlineSelectCreate (searchable dropdown + inline creation). See `asciiDiagrams.md §UX Patterns` for full layouts.

| # | Task | Complexity | Status | Session | Notes |
|---|------|-----------|--------|---------|-------|
| UX1 | `FormShell` — full-width side panel component | M | ✅ | Session 100 | New `appkit/src/features/shell/FormShell.tsx`. Full-viewport-width overlay that slides in from the right. Props: `title`, `breadcrumb`, `onClose`, `onSave`, `onPublish`, `sections[]` (for left nav anchor links), `previewSlot`, `children`. Renders: sticky top bar (breadcrumb, title, [Preview ↗], [Save Draft], [Publish/Update]), optional left section nav (200px, scrolls into view), scrollable body, sticky bottom bar ([Discard], [Save Draft], [Publish →]). Mobile: left nav becomes horizontal tab strip. Keyboard trap + Esc with unsaved-changes confirm dialog. Backdrop dims page behind (no page reload). Exports `useFormShell()` hook for dirty state tracking. |
| UX2 | `QuickFormDrawer` — narrow ≤ 6-field action drawer | S | ✅ | Session 100 | New `appkit/src/features/shell/QuickFormDrawer.tsx`. 400px right-anchored overlay (uses existing `SideDrawer` primitive). Props: `title`, `fields: FieldDef[]`, `onSubmit`, `onCancel`, `defaultValues`. Auto-renders form fields from `FieldDef[]` array (text, select, toggle, date, number). Inline error display below each field. [Cancel] + [Create/Save →] buttons in sticky footer. Used for: address add/edit, coupon create, tag add, status change, price edit, nav item edit, review reply. |
| UX3 | `StepForm` — multi-step wizard inside FormShell | M | ✅ | Session 100 | New `appkit/src/features/shell/StepForm.tsx`. Renders inside FormShell body, replacing section nav for CREATE flows. Props: `steps: Array<{ label, component, validate? }>`, `onComplete`, `formId` (for localStorage progress). Step indicator bar (numbered circles: ✓ done / ◑ current / ○ locked). Per-step `validate()` gate before advancing — shows inline error if invalid. Bottom bar CTA labels change per step (`Next: Media →` / `← Back: Basic` / `Publish Now ✓`). Progress auto-saved to `localStorage[formId]` on each step advance. |
| UX4 | `PreviewPane` — in-panel item preview | M | 🔜 | post-alpha | [👁 Preview] button in FormShell top bar and left nav. Replaces panel body with a read-only render of the item using current draft form values. Draft banner at top ("Not visible to buyers until published"). All interactive actions (Buy/Cart/Bid/Reserve) receive `disabled` prop → greyed out + tooltip. "← Back to Edit" restores form body. Secondary mode: "Open in new tab ↗" — POSTs draft to `/api/preview` → short-lived token → `/preview?token={x}` renders full public layout. Applies to: ProductDetailPageView, AuctionDetailPageView, PreOrderDetailPageView, BlogPostView, EventDetailView. |
| UX5 | `MediaPickerDrawer` — fast media select/upload/reorder | L | 🔜 | post-alpha | Full-viewport overlay (above FormShell) for all media upload fields. Features: grid of existing uploads (24/page, paginated); search by filename; filter by type (image/video/document) and date; multi-select via checkboxes; upload new via drag+drop zone (stores to `tmp/` first, shows upload progress bar); reorder selected set via drag handles (determines image order on product page); right-click/⋮ menu per tile: [★ Set as main] [🗑 Delete] [📋 Copy URL] [🔍 Full-size]. `[tmp]` badge on files uploaded this session. On form Submit → API moves `tmp/{file}` to `products/{id}/{file}`. Abandoned `tmp/` files auto-deleted after 24 h by Cloud Function. Returns `string[]` of selected URLs to calling form field via callback. Replaces existing `MediaPickerModal` (I4) which lacks drag-reorder and tmp/ handling. |
| UX6 | Apply FormShell + StepForm to all 3 product forms | L | ✅ | Session 100 | Standard product create (5 steps: Basic/Media/Pricing/Shipping/SEO). Auction create (6 steps: +Auction Settings as step 3). Pre-order create (6 steps: +Pre-Order Settings as step 3). All product edits use FormShell with left section nav (same sections, jump to any). MediaPickerDrawer wired to image and video fields. PreviewPane available at all times in top bar + on final step. Listing type selector at top of create flow: [+ New Product ▾] → Standard / Auction / Pre-order. |
| UX7 | Apply FormShell + QuickFormDrawer to store-side forms | M | ✅ | Session 80 | Shipping config (SellerShippingView) and payout settings (SellerPayoutSettingsView) use StackedViewShell full-form pattern. Store profile edit uses SellerStorefrontView with useFormShell. StoreAddressSelectorCreate handles pickup address inline create (O3). UX9 InlineSelectCreate deferred post-alpha. |
| UX8 | Admin inline quick-edit actions via QuickFormDrawer | M | ⏳ | post-alpha | Replace "click row → navigate to full edit page" for simple admin actions with QuickFormDrawer: quick status update (product, order, event), quick price edit, quick stock quantity, quick feature toggle (isFeatured, isPromoted). Row ⋮ menu → opens QuickFormDrawer instead of full page navigate. Keeps admin in the list view — faster moderation workflow. |
| UX9 | `InlineSelectCreate` — searchable dropdown with inline quick-create | M | 🔜 | post-alpha | **New pattern** for every "select existing or create new" field across all forms. A searchable combobox where the last option is always [+ Create "xxx"]. Selecting that option opens a `QuickFormDrawer` scoped to that resource. On QuickFormDrawer save → new item auto-selected in the dropdown and drawer closes. Uses: (1) **Category** — search/select category, [+ Create "Sports Cards"] → opens category QuickForm (name, parent, slug-auto). (2) **Brand** — search/select brand, [+ Create "Kotobukiya"] → brand QuickForm (name, country, website). (3) **Tag / Keyword** — multi-select tag input, [+ Add "psa-10"] → saves tag inline, no drawer needed (simple text add). (4) **Product Feature** — bulleted list with [+ Add feature] → text input inline (no drawer). (5) **Delivery Address** (checkout) — dropdown of saved addresses, [+ Add new address] → address QuickFormDrawer. (6) **Pickup Address** (product shipping) — dropdown of store addresses, [+ Add new store address] → store address QuickFormDrawer. (7) **Coupon** (checkout) — search/apply coupon code, [+ Create new coupon] → coupon QuickFormDrawer (admin/store only). (8) **Sub-category parent** (admin category edit) — parent category selector, [+ Create parent] → category QuickForm. See `asciiDiagrams.md §UX > InlineSelectCreate` for diagram. Note: H1 (✅ done) covers the base component — UX9 wires it to QuickFormDrawer and applies it to all the above fields consistently. |

Max 20MB. Use in: order invoice upload (VC2), seller payout proof upload (VB3), product spec-sheet attachment field. Store under `documents/` path prefix instead of `media/`. |
| I8 | YouTube + external media URL support in all media fields | M | ✅ | Session 64 | `MediaField` type extended with `source?: "upload"\|"youtube"\|"external"` + `youtubeId?: string`. `MediaUploadField` gets `showYoutube` + `showExternal` props + tab switcher + `extractYouTubeId()` helper. |
| INFRA1 | firebase-reset.mjs dry-run crash — `.count()` not available in firebase-admin v10 | S | ✅ | Session 76-infra (2026-05-10) | `summarizeFirestore()` called `collectionRef.count().get()` which is a Firestore v11+ aggregate API. appkit uses `firebase-admin@^10.3.0`. Fixed in `appkit/scripts/firebase-reset.mjs`: replaced `.count().get()` with `.get()` and `.size` on the snapshot. |
| INFRA2 | firebase-delete-indexes.mjs — new utility to delete all Firestore composite indexes via REST API | S | ✅ | Session 76-infra (2026-05-10) | Created `appkit/scripts/firebase-delete-indexes.mjs`. Uses firebase-tools OAuth refresh token (from `~/.config/configstore/firebase-tools.json`) + client credentials to get a fresh access token, then calls `GET /v1/projects/{project}/databases/(default)/collectionGroups/-/indexes` to list all indexes and `DELETE` each by resource name. Required because `firebase deploy --only firestore:indexes` gets 409 "index already exists" when partial deploys leave indexes in CREATING state. Also fixed duplicate `faqs` indexes (`isPinned,priority,order` × 2 and `isActive,createdAt` × 2) in `appkit/firebase/base/firestore.indexes.json`. Run before `npm run firebase:deploy` when 409 errors persist. |
| I7 | Media CDN proxy with configurable watermarking | L | ⏳ | | NEW: `src/app/api/media/[...slug]/route.ts` — Node.js runtime (`sharp` requires Node, not Edge). **Server handles all image delivery** — client never fetches from Firebase Storage directly. Flow: request → fetch original via Admin SDK (Storage rules: private, no `allUsers` read) → read watermark config from `site_settings/singleton` (cached in-memory, TTL 60s) → apply watermark via `sharp` → respond with `Cache-Control: public, max-age=86400, s-maxage=604800, immutable`. Vercel CDN caches per slug. **Watermark config** (stored in `site_settings/singleton`): `watermarkType: "text" | "image"`, `watermarkText` (default `"letitrip.in"`), `watermarkImageUrl` (proxy URL of uploaded watermark image), `watermarkSize` (0–100, % of target image width; aspect ratio of both target and watermark preserved). At 100% the watermark spans the full image width. If no config or size=0 defaults to text "letitrip.in" at 30%. **All Firestore image URL fields must use `/media/<slug>` path** — never raw `firebasestorage.googleapis.com/…` URLs. Seed data URL fields updated to `/media/` scheme. Video: thumbnails watermarked via proxy; player renders CSS overlay badge (client-side). Baked-in video watermark deferred (FFmpeg needed). Depends on VA8 for the settings UI. |

### P23–P31: Seed Data Scale Expansion + New Collections *(ordered by dependency)*

> All P23+ tasks require P11–P22 done. Media URLs must use official brand sites, Wikipedia Commons, or Pokémon TCG API — no Unsplash placeholder landscapes. YouTube IDs must be real unboxing/review videos. All seed data must pass Zod validation against the same schemas used in production forms. PII fields (name, email, phone, address) must be masked in the seeded DB records (encrypt or hash) with a way to view unmasked data in the SeedPanel.
>
> **⚠️ J13 seed rule (enforced forever):** Every standard product document MUST have `isAuction: false` AND `isPreOrder: false` explicitly set. Every auction document MUST have `isAuction: true`. Every pre-order MUST have `isPreOrder: true`. Firestore `where("isAuction", "==", false)` does NOT match documents where the field is absent — this caused the products listing to return zero results in Session 76-infra. Required composite indexes `(status, isAuction, createdAt)` and `(status, isAuction, isPreOrder, createdAt)` are in `appkit/firebase/base/firestore.indexes.json` — do not remove them.

| P31 | Seed runner — Zod validation, error handling, PII masking, dry-run diff | M | ⏳ | | **(A) Zod validation**: Before any `batch.set()` in the seed runner, validate each document against the same Zod schema used in the admin/seller form for that collection (import from `appkit/src/features/*/schemas/`). Validation failures surface as `{ status: "error", id, detail: zodError.format() }` in the per-collection result — never silently drop bad docs. Add a `STRICT_VALIDATION=true` env flag that throws on first validation error (for CI), vs the default behavior of skipping bad docs and continuing. **(B) PII masking**: Users seed data — emails hashed to `sha256(email)@demo.letitrip.in` in the seeded document; phone stored as `+91-XXXX-XX${last4}`; fullName on addresses stored as first name + last initial (e.g. "Ravi K."). Add an optional `?unmask=true` query param to `GET /api/demo/seed` response that returns real PII values — protected by `x-demo-seed-key` header matching `DEMO_SEED_KEY` env var. SeedPanel UI adds a "Show PII" toggle that re-fetches with `x-demo-seed-key`. **(C) Dry-run diff**: When `dryRun=true`, the seed runner computes a diff of what would change — `{ toCreate: id[], toUpdate: id[], toSkip: id[], toDelete?: id[] }` per collection. The per-collection result in SeedPanel shows this diff in the expanded accordion card under "Dry Run Preview" section. **(D) Error handling**: Wrap every Firestore batch in try/catch with retry (1 retry on network errors). Auth user creation failures are non-fatal if the user already exists (use `getUser` + `updateUser` fallback). Log each failed document ID + error message to `console.error` and surface in the SeedPanel accordion card's error section. |

## Tier Q — Query/Sieve via Firebase Function

> **SIEVE SYSTEM DESIGN DECISIONS (2026-05-06)**
>
> **Text search (`q=`)**: Instead of a separate JS pass, define per-collection searchable fields (e.g. `title`, `description`, `tags`). The `listingProcessor` translates `q=VALUE` into a Firestore `where(field, '>=', value).where(field, '<=', value+'')` range query on each searchable field, combined with the `f=` filters in one Firestore call. This avoids the JS in-memory pass entirely. Each collection registers its searchable fields in a config map inside the function.
>
> **Caching**: Use Firebase's built-in Firestore SDK cache (`enableIndexedDbPersistence` on client) + Cloud Function responses cached via `Cache-Control: public, max-age=60, s-maxage=120` headers. For listing pages served via Vercel, CDN caches the response; the Firebase Function is only called on cache miss.
>
> **Pagination + Infinite Scroll**: Cursor-based pagination (startAfter lastDoc) prevents page drift. Function returns an opaque `cursor` token alongside items. The same cursor mechanism powers two display modes via a `mode` prop on listing views:
> - `"pages"` mode: traditional numbered pagination; cursor stored per-page in a Map so forward/back navigation reuses cached cursors.
> - `"infinite"` mode: IntersectionObserver fires when user scrolls near bottom; next batch fetched using returned cursor and appended to list.
> **Default**: public listing pages (products, auctions, pre-orders, stores) use `"infinite"`. Admin/store data tables use `"pages"`.
>
> **Filter format**: Standard sievejs expressions — `fieldName==value`, `fieldName>=value`, etc. No shorthand aliases.

| # | Task | Complexity | Status | Part | Notes |
|---|------|-----------|--------|------|-------|
| Q1 | `listingProcessor` Firebase HTTPS Function | M | ⏳ | | File: `functions/src/callable/listing-processor.ts`. Input: `{ collection, q?, f?, s?, p?, ps?, cursor? }`. Text search via per-collection field config (range queries, no JS pass). Cursor-based pagination. Cache-Control header on response. Set `minInstances: 1`. Returns `{ items, total, page, pageSize, cursor, hasMore }`. |
| Q2 | Standardise listing API query param names | S | ⏳ | | All `/api/products`, `/api/pre-orders`, `/api/stores` routes accept short names: `f=` (filters), `s=` (sort), `p=` (page), `ps=` (pageSize), `q=` (search), `cursor=` (pagination cursor). Map internally. Keep old param names working for backwards compat. |
| Q3 | Delegate listing API routes to `listingProcessor` Firebase Function | M | ⏳ | | Replace direct Sieve calls in `/api/products/route.ts` and `/api/pre-orders/route.ts` with HTTP calls to `listingProcessor`. Use Firebase Admin SDK server-side. Vercel route becomes thin proxy. |
| Q4 | Update appkit listing views for new param names + cursor pagination | S | ⏳ | | `AuctionsListView`, `ProductsIndexPageView`, `PreOrdersListView`, `StoreProductsPageView`: read `f`, `s`, `p`, `ps`, `cursor` from `searchParams`. Store cursor Map for forward/back navigation. |
| Q5 | Firestore composite indexes for common filter+sort combos | S | ⏳ | | Add to `firestore.indexes.json`: `(category, price)`, `(brandSlug, createdAt)`, `(storeId, status)`, `(isAuction, auctionEndDate)`, `(isPromoted, createdAt)`, `(featured, createdAt)`. Deploy with `firebase deploy --only firestore:indexes`. |
| Q6 | Infinite scroll on public listing pages | M | ⏳ | | Add `useInfiniteScroll` hook in appkit: wraps `IntersectionObserver` on a sentinel `div` at list bottom; on intersect fetches next cursor batch and appends to items state. Wire into `ProductsIndexPageView`, `AuctionsListView`, `PreOrdersListView`, `StoreProductsPageView` as `mode="infinite"`. Show skeleton cards while loading next batch. "Back to top" button appears after 2 pages loaded. Admin/store tables keep `mode="pages"`. |

## Tier CU — Coupon Abuse Prevention

> These bugs were discovered and fixed in Session 77 (2026-05-10). The core tracking infrastructure already existed in the schema; the gaps were in the runtime wiring.

| # | Task | Complexity | Status | Notes |
|---|------|-----------|--------|-------|
| CU1 | Call `applyCoupon()` at checkout to persist usage | S | ✅ | `src/app/api/checkout/route.ts` — imports `couponsRepository`, accumulates per-coupon discount+orderIds across all order groups, fires `applyCoupon()` fire-and-forget after orders created. Without this, `usage.currentUsage` and `users/{uid}/couponUsage/{couponId}` were never written, allowing infinite coupon reuse. |
| CU2 | Fix `getUserCouponUsageCount()` — returned 0 or 1 only | S | ✅ | `appkit/src/features/promotions/repository/coupons.repository.ts` — changed `return doc.exists ? 1 : 0` to read actual `usageCount` field. Required for `perUserLimit > 1` to work correctly. |
| CU3 | Fix `applyCoupon()` — overwrote usage doc, empty code | S | ✅ | Same file — changed `batch.set()` overwrite to `set({merge:true})` with `increment(usageCount)` + `arrayUnion(orderIds)`. Added `couponCode` param (was hardcoded `""`). Added `arrayUnion` import. Signature: `applyCoupon(couponId, couponCode, userId, orderIds[], discountAmount)`. |
| CU4 | Enforce 100% cap on percentage discounts at creation | S | ✅ | `src/app/api/admin/coupons/route.ts` — added `.superRefine()` to `couponCreateSchema`: rejects `type==="percentage" && discount.value > 100` with a typed Zod issue. |
| CU5 | Enforce 100% cap on percentage discounts at update | S | ✅ | `src/app/api/admin/coupons/[id]/route.ts` and `src/app/api/store/coupons/[id]/route.ts` — fetch existing coupon, reject 422 if `type==="percentage" && incoming discount.value > 100`. |
| CU6 | Seed `users/{uid}/couponUsage/` subcollection | S | ✅ | New file `appkit/src/seed/coupon-usage-seed-data.ts` — 6 realistic records (buyers who used WELCOME10, POKEMON25, FREESHIP999, BEYARENA20, PALACE15, TOKYOTOYS10). Wired into `src/app/api/demo/seed/route.ts` as new `couponUsage` collection type with load/delete/count handlers. |

This prevents duplicate creation and speeds up future sessions. |

## Tier GP — Grouped Listings *(standard products + pre-orders only; no auctions)*

> A "group" is a parent product linked to 1–N child products (e.g., "Human Toy Complete Set" links to "head", "legs", "arms" as separate fully independent listings). Depth is exactly 1 — no grandchildren. Each member has its own title, slug, price, images, and checkout flow. The group thread is visible as a collapsible "Show group (N items)" panel on every member's detail page.

| # | Task | Complexity | Status | Part | Notes |
|---|------|-----------|--------|------|-------|
| GP1 | Grouped listings schema + `ShowGroupSection` component | M | ✅ | | **Schema** (`appkit/src/features/products/schemas/firestore.ts`): add to `ProductDocument`: `groupId?: string` (= parent slug; same on parent + all children), `isGroupParent?: boolean`, `groupParentSlug?: string` (null on parent; parent's slug on children), `groupChildSlugs?: string[]` (parent only), `groupTitle?: string` (e.g. "Human Toy Complete Set"). Slug convention: parent = `product-human-toy`; children append part name (`product-human-toy-head`). **New component** `appkit/src/features/products/components/ShowGroupSection.tsx` — receives `groupId` + `currentSlug` + `isParent` props; renders nothing if `groupId` absent. Fetches all products/pre-orders with matching `groupId`. **Parent view**: collapsible panel "Parts in this group (N)". **Child view**: collapsible panel "Part of: [groupTitle]". Both collapsed by default. **Card style**: small circular thumbnail cards (~64 px) in a `HorizontalScroller`; cards are selectable — clicking navigates to that member's detail page; current product has a highlighted ring border. Parent card shown first with a "Set" badge. **"View whole group →" button** opens a `Modal` (or `SideDrawer` if ≥ 5 parts) with a table — columns: thumbnail (click to expand image preview), name, price, condition, "View" link. Standard products + pre-orders only. **Placement**: injected via a new `renderGroupSection` render prop on `ProductDetailView` and the pre-order equivalent — rendered between the buy-box/actions area and the TABS row (NOT in `belowFold`). `npx tsc --noEmit` → 0 errors. |
| GP2 | Edit-screen "Group settings" panel + inline child creation + link-existing | M | ✅ | | Depends on GP1. Add collapsible **"Group settings"** section to `AdminProductEditorView` and seller `ProductForm.tsx`. Hidden on auction forms. **Three states**: *(1) Not in a group* — "Start a group" button → sets `isGroupParent: true`, `groupId: this.slug`. *(2) This is the group parent* — shows `groupTitle` input; lists children (thumbnail, title, price, condition, "Unlink" button in batch write); **"Add child listing"** button → modal with **two tabs**: **Tab 1 — Create new child**: minimal form with only the fields that differ (title, slug auto-suggested as `parent-slug-[part]`, price, short description, condition, images via MediaUploadField); all other fields (category, brand, storeId, tags, shippingInfo, returnPolicy) shown as read-only "Inherited from parent" badges; on save: creates new product doc with inherited fields + minimal changes; updates parent `groupChildSlugs` atomically; toast; "Need more control? Edit the full listing after saving" note. **Tab 2 — Link existing**: searchable `DynamicSelect` across products + pre-orders by title or slug; validates: candidate not already in a group, not an auction; on confirm: batch-writes `groupId`/`groupParentSlug` onto the linked listing + adds its slug to parent `groupChildSlugs`. Also: "Dissolve group" button (confirm required) → batch-clears all group fields on parent + all children. *(3) This is a child* — "Part of: [groupTitle]" read-only banner with link to parent edit page; "Leave group" button (confirm). All multi-doc writes are atomic batch. |

## Tier SC — Sub-listing Categories *(all listing types: products, auctions, pre-orders)*

> A "sub-listing category" is a named bucket (e.g., "Base Set 1 Charizard 108/120") that groups multiple independent listings of the same real-world collectible with different conditions, grades, prices, and sellers. Each listing is still its own full product/auction/pre-order — the sub-listing category is just the thread linking them. The public page shows all members. The detail page shows a collapsible horizontal scroller "More listings in: [name]".

| # | Task | Complexity | Status | Part | Notes |
|---|------|-----------|--------|------|-------|
| SC1 | Sub-listing categories — schema + repository + API routes | M | ✅ | | **New Firestore collection**: `sublisting_categories`. **`SublistingCategoryDocument`** type (new file `appkit/src/features/products/schemas/sublisting-categories.ts` or add to categories schema): `id: string` (= slug), `slug: string` (prefix: `sublisting-`), `name: string`, `itemCode?: string` (e.g. "108/120", "PSA-10"), `description?: string`, `coverImage?: string` (`/media/<slug>` proxy URL), `productCount: number` (maintained via batch write), `createdAt: Date`, `updatedAt: Date`, `createdBy: string`. **New field on `ProductDocument`** (and auction/pre-order if separate schemas): `sublistingCategoryId?: string` (a listing belongs to at most 1 sub-listing category). **`SublistingCategoriesRepository`** — same pattern as `CategoriesRepository`: `findById`, `findBySlug`, `list(model)` (Sieve pagination), `create`, `update`, `delete`, `getListingsByCategoryId(id, limit?)` (returns products + auctions + pre-orders with matching `sublistingCategoryId`, ordered by price, default limit 10). **API routes**: `GET /api/admin/sublisting-categories` (list + search), `POST /api/admin/sublisting-categories` (create), `GET /api/admin/sublisting-categories/[id]` (get one), `PUT /api/admin/sublisting-categories/[id]` (update), `DELETE /api/admin/sublisting-categories/[id]` (delete — unlinks all members first by batch-clearing their `sublistingCategoryId`), `GET /api/sublisting-categories/[slug]` (public — returns category + first 20 listings), `GET /api/sublisting-categories/[slug]/listings` (paginated public listings). Slug prefix `sublisting-` registered in Tier 0-pre table. After: `npx tsc --noEmit` → 0 errors. |
| SC2 | Admin CRUD for sub-listing categories | M | ✅ | | Depends on SC1. **List view** `AdminSublistingCategoriesView` (`appkit/src/features/admin/components/`): columns — name, itemCode, productCount, createdAt, "Edit"/"Delete" `RowActionMenu`. Uses `AdminListingScaffold` (existing). Search + pagination via `useUrlTable`. **Editor view** `AdminSublistingCategoryEditorView`: form fields — name (text input, required), itemCode (text input, optional, e.g. card set code), description (textarea), coverImage (`MediaUploadField`). Save via `POST /api/admin/sublisting-categories` (create) or `PUT /api/admin/sublisting-categories/[id]` (update). Uses `SideDrawer` or dedicated page. Delete via `ConfirmDeleteModal`. **Routes**: `/admin/sublisting-categories` (list) + `/admin/sublisting-categories/new` + `/admin/sublisting-categories/[id]/edit`. Add to **admin navigation sidebar**. All actions use `useToast`. |
| SC3 | `sublistingCategoryId` field on all listing forms + `SublistingCarouselSection` component | M | ✅ | | Depends on SC1. **Form field** (this is the ONLY way listings are linked to sub-listing categories — no central "assign products" UI): add "Sub-listing category" `DynamicSelect` to product/pre-order/auction create+edit forms, pulling from `/api/admin/sublisting-categories`. Works exactly like the existing category field — pick existing or create inline (small modal: name + itemCode inputs). Selecting None clears the field. **New component** `appkit/src/features/products/components/SublistingCarouselSection.tsx`: receives `sublistingCategoryId` prop; renders nothing if absent. Fetches first 10 listings with matching `sublistingCategoryId` from public API. Renders as **collapsible panel** "More listings like this: [category name]" — collapsed by default. Inside: `HorizontalScroller` of small **circular thumbnail cards** (~64 px); per card: circular image, product name (2-line truncation), price chip; clicking navigates to that listing's detail page; current listing is highlighted with a ring border. "View all (N) →" link → `/sublisting-categories/[slug]`. **Placement**: injected via a new `renderSublistingSection` render prop on `ProductDetailView`, `AuctionDetailView`, and the pre-order equivalent — rendered between the buy-box/actions area and the TABS row (NOT in `belowFold`). `npx tsc --noEmit` → 0 errors. |
| SC4 | Public sub-listing category page + routes | M | ✅ | | Depends on SC1+SC3. **New page** `src/app/[locale]/sublisting-categories/[slug]/page.tsx` — server component: fetches category + paginated listings via public API. Renders: category header (name, itemCode, coverImage, description, `productCount` badge), then paginated listing grid reusing existing `ProductCard`/`AuctionCard`/`PreOrderCard`. Breadcrumb: Home → Sub-listing Categories → [Name]. `generateMetadata` for SEO (og:title, og:description, og:image via coverImage). Add `ROUTES.PUBLIC.SUBLISTING_CATEGORIES` + `ROUTES.PUBLIC.SUBLISTING_CATEGORY(slug)` to constants. No-listing empty state must render without crash. |

## Tier SR — Global Search Redesign

> Replace the tab-based `/search/[query]/tab/[tab]/sort/[sortKey]/page/[page]` flow with direct resource-type navigation. The search bar gets an inline resource type selector; submitting navigates to that resource's own public listing page with `?q=` pre-filled. Zero fuzzy search, zero third-party dependency — all suggestions come from existing Firestore data.

| # | Task | Complexity | Status | Part | Notes |

Search placeholder updated to "Search collectibles…". `npx tsc --noEmit` → 0 errors both repos. |
| SR2 | Simplify / redirect the old `/search` page | S | ✅ | 2026-05-10 | `/search/page.tsx` rewritten as pure redirect handler: reads `?q=` and `?type=`, validates type against `VALID_TYPES` set, redirects to listing page. `metadata.robots = noindex`. Legacy `/search/[searchSlug]/tab/[tab]/sort/[sortKey]/page/[page]/page.tsx` rewritten as `permanentRedirect` — preserves tab→route mapping (auctions→/auctions, pre-orders→/pre-orders, all/products→/products). `SearchResultsClient.tsx` is now dead code (not deleted — no destructive deletes without user confirmation). |

After SR1 nav fix (`?q=` not `?search=`), all toolbar inputs correctly pre-fill. ⚠️ FAQs: uses `FAQPageView` (static server component from translation messages) — no search toolbar; `?q=` URL param is silently accepted but has no effect. ## Tier ARCH — Store Identity Architecture *(storeId/storeName public; sellerId = internal auth only)*

> **Core rule**: The store is the public identity on LetiTrip — not the individual seller user behind it. Public-facing APIs, UI cards, detail pages, cart items, and profiles must show `storeId` / `storeName` / `storeSlug`. The Firebase UID of the store owner (`sellerId` internally) is an auth/internal field only — it must never appear in a public API response or client-rendered prop. Admin views may additionally display `ownerId` (display alias for `sellerId` in admin context). Server-only code (checkout, analytics, payout calculation, authorization) may continue using `sellerId` for auth logic without change.
>
> **SideDrawer vs Modal rule** (enforced from this tier forward): 0 fields → `ConfirmDeleteModal`; 1–2 fields → `Modal`; 3+ fields → `SideDrawer`.
>
> **User roles** (public 3-tier): `user` (basic buyer) | `seller` (has ≥1 store) | `admin` (platform admin). `moderator` is an internal sub-role of admin.

| # | Task | Complexity | Status | Part | Notes |
|---|------|-----------|--------|------|-------|
| ARCH1 | Public API sanitization: strip sellerId from product/review/order public responses | M | ⏳ | | `/api/products/route.ts` — delete `sellerId` key before returning items. `/api/reviews/*` public list — same. Public order listing — strip. Server-side auth code keeps `sellerId` unchanged. |
| ARCH2 | Cart items: sellerId/sellerName → storeId/storeName | M | ✅ | Session 81 | Cart/Order/Coupon/Offer/Payout schemas all migrated. Checkout two-step shipping lookup (storeId→ownerId→user). Bid guard fixed. All seed data updated. All repositories renamed (findBySeller→findByStore etc.). ProductItem type gained storeName. Both appkit and main app pass tsc --noEmit 0 errors. |
| ARCH3 | Reviews schema: remove sellerId field | S | ✅ | Session 80 | Removed `sellerId` from `ReviewListParams` (types/index.ts), `reviewSchema` + `reviewListParamsSchema` (schemas/index.ts → replaced with `storeSlug`/`storeId`), `useReviews.ts` hook. `review-actions.ts` already used `storeId: product.storeId`. Seed data maps `sellerId` → `{storeId, storeName}` via `SELLER_STORE` lookup at export time. |
| ARCH4 | Admin payouts: storeId/storeName identity + mark-paid + CSV export | M | ✅ | Session 72 | `AdminPayoutsView`: storeName/storeId identity (sellerName fallback until ARCH8); RowActionMenu "Mark paid" → Modal (1 field: transactionId); Export CSV actionsSlot button downloads via GET /api/admin/payouts/export; PATCH /api/admin/payouts/[id] for mark-paid. NEW: `src/app/api/admin/payouts/export/route.ts` — text/csv, columns: id/storeId/storeName/amount/status/transactionId/periodStart/periodEnd/createdAt. ADMIN_ENDPOINTS.PAYOUTS_EXPORT added. |
| ARCH5 | Admin payouts weekly batch: group by storeId not sellerId | S | ✅ | Session 81 | `/api/admin/payouts/weekly/route.ts`: payoutData.sellerId → storeId, already grouped by storeId from orders. Done as part of ARCH2 migration. |
| ARCH6 | Public product cards + detail pages: show store identity | M | ⏳ | | Everywhere a product card or detail page shows "seller" info, switch to store: `storeName` + link to `/stores/{storeSlug}`. Affects: `ProductCard`, `AuctionCard`, `PreorderCard`, product detail page. Never show `sellerName` or `sellerId` to public users. |
| ARCH7 | Seller profile page: store-first identity; admin view shows ownerId | M | ⏳ | | Public `/profile/{userId}` for a seller: show store card prominently (storeName, storeSlug, logo) — not user bio name. Admin `/admin/users/{id}` detail: show `ownerId` (Firebase UID) alongside `storeId` for the stores they own. |
| ARCH8 | Seed data unification: all collections → store identity | L | ✅ | Session 81 | Done as part of ARCH2 migration: payouts, orders, cart, coupons, all product seeds (letitrip-official, anime-figures, beyblade, hot-wheels, transformers, retro-gaming, cosplay-accessories) all migrated to storeId/storeName, storeId prefix corrected (store- prefix). |
| ARCH9 | Chat room schema: rename sellerId → ownerId | S | ✅ | S1 2026-05-11 | Renamed `sellerId`→`ownerId`, `sellerName`→`ownerName` across: `appkit/src/features/admin/schemas/firestore.ts` (ChatRoomDocument interface, CHAT_ROOM_FIELDS, CHAT_ROOM_INDEXED_FIELDS, DEFAULT_CHAT_ROOM_DATA, chatRoomQueryHelpers), `chat.repository.ts`, `chat-actions.ts`, `useChat.ts`, `src/app/api/chat/route.ts`, `src/actions/chat.actions.ts`. appkit dist rebuilt. 0 TSC errors both repos. |

## Tier SEO — Lighthouse & Search Engine Optimisation *(post-alpha, before RBAC)*

> **Goal**: Achieve Lighthouse Performance ≥ 90 and eliminate crawlability gaps on all public pages. The alpha release built a full CMS-driven homepage and product catalogue, but the rendering strategy leaves most content invisible to crawlers and degrades Core Web Vitals. This tier fixes that without touching any admin, store, or user dashboard functionality.
>
> **Root problems identified (2026-05-10 audit)**:
> 1. Every homepage section component (`FeaturedProductsSection`, `ShopByCategorySection`, `BrandsSection`, etc.) is `"use client"` and fetches its own data via hooks — Googlebot sees empty skeletons in initial HTML; product/auction/brand/category content is absent from the page source.
> 2. `HeroCarousel` receives `initialSlides` as a prop from the server but renders everything client-side — the first-slide image (the LCP element) cannot be `priority`-loaded; crawlers get no slide content.
> 3. `ProductGrid.tsx` (lines ~100 and ~413) uses `style={{ backgroundImage: url(...) }}` — images are not optimised by Next.js (no WebP/AVIF, no `srcset`, no lazy-load control, no LCP eligibility).
> 4. JSON-LD helpers (`productJsonLd`, `auctionJsonLd`, `blogPostJsonLd`, etc.) exist in `appkit/src/seo/json-ld.ts` but are called nowhere — no rich snippets (price, ratings, breadcrumbs, article byline) appear in Google search results.
> 5. 15+ public pages (`/sellers`, `/help`, `/contact`, `/how-*/`, `/fees`, `/security`, etc.) export no `metadata` at all — no title, description, or Open Graph tags.
> 6. Paginated and filtered routes (`/search/[...]/page/[n]`, `/categories/[slug]/tab/.../page/[page]`) have no canonical URL — Google may penalise for duplicate content.
>
> **Constraints**: All fixes are in `appkit/src/` or `src/` only. No admin, store, or user dashboard pages are touched. No Firestore schemas change. The carousel and homepage section CMS (CF1, HS1–HS5) remain exactly as-is — only the public render path changes. VD3 is subsumed into SEO5.
>
> **Do SEO1 → SEO2 → SEO3 → SEO4 → SEO5 → SEO6 → SEO7 in order** (each is independently deployable but they compound — do not skip).

| # | Task | Complexity | Status | Notes |
|---|------|-----------|--------|-------|
| SEO1 | Homepage sections: SSR data hydration so carousel content appears in initial HTML | L | ✅ | Session 82 | **Problem**: `FeaturedProductsSection`, `FeaturedAuctionsSection`, `FeaturedPreOrdersSection`, `FeaturedStoresSection`, `ShopByCategorySection`, `BrandsSection`, `BlogArticlesSection`, `EventsSection` all fetch their own data client-side via hooks (`useFeaturedProducts`, `useFeaturedAuctions`, etc.). Googlebot sees empty skeletons; product/auction/brand/category content is invisible without JS. **Fix — three parts**: **(1) `MarketplaceHomepageView.tsx`** (already a server component): after the existing `Promise.all` for sections + FAQs, add a second parallel fetch that reads enabled section types from `orderedSections` and fetches only what is configured — e.g. if a `products` section is present call `productsRepository.getFeatured({ maxCount: cfg.maxCount ?? 8, filterByBrand: cfg.filterByBrand })`. Collect results into a typed `SectionData` map keyed by section id. Pass this map as a new `sectionData` prop to `renderSection`. **(2) `section-renderer.tsx`**: each resource section branch (products, auctions, pre-orders, stores, categories, brands, blog, events) reads its preloaded items from `sectionData[section.id]` and passes them as an `initialItems` prop to the section component. **(3) Section components**: add `initialItems?: T[]` prop. When provided, skip the client-side hook on first render and use `initialItems` instead; keep the hook for client-side refresh/stale-while-revalidate. `HorizontalScroller` already renders all children into the DOM — no change needed there. **Result**: all product/auction/brand/store/category cards appear in initial HTML; carousel JS activates on hydration. `npx tsc --noEmit` → 0 errors in both repos. |
| SEO2 | HeroCarousel: render first slide in SSR HTML + `priority` image for LCP | M | ✅ | Session 82 — `initialSlides` already threaded from server; first slide background uses `priority={slideIndex===0}`. Client component rendered to HTML by Next.js SSR. | **Problem**: `HeroCarousel` is `"use client"` and renders all slides after hydration, even though it already receives `initialSlides` from the server. The hero background image (largest above-the-fold element) is invisible to crawlers and cannot be `priority`-loaded. **Fix**: add a static first-slide fallback inside `HeroCarousel` that is visible on the first server-rendered paint before JS hydrates. Strategy — render the first slide from `initialSlides[0]` as a plain `<div>` with `<MediaImage priority sizes="100vw">` for the background, the slide heading, subheading, and CTA buttons as real DOM nodes. Once `useEffect` fires on mount, replace this static fallback with the full interactive carousel and hide the fallback via CSS. The static fallback is `aria-hidden="true"` on mount (screen readers should use the live carousel), but its text content is in the DOM for Googlebot. First slide `MediaImage` always gets `priority={true}` and `sizes="100vw"`. Subsequent slides remain lazy. **Result**: LCP image is identifiable + downloadable immediately; first-slide text and CTAs appear in page source; Google indexes carousel content. `npx tsc --noEmit` → 0 errors. |
| SEO3 | Product card images: replace `background-image` inline style with `<MediaImage>` | S | ✅ | Session 82 | **File**: `appkit/src/features/products/components/ProductGrid.tsx` — two instances: line ~100 (standard card image) and line ~413 (compact/list view card image). **Fix**: replace `<div role="img" style={{ backgroundImage: \`url(${product.mainImage})\` }} />` with `<MediaImage src={product.mainImage} fill alt={product.title} sizes="(max-width: 640px) 50vw, (max-width: 1024px) 33vw, 25vw" />` inside the existing card image container div (add `position: relative` to the wrapper if not already present). Accept an `index` prop from the parent grid and pass `priority={index < 4}` to `MediaImage` so the first four above-fold cards are LCP-eligible with eager loading. The existing `bg-cover bg-center` classes move to the `MediaImage` via `className` and `style={{ objectFit: "cover" }}`. Fallback (no image): keep the existing gradient div. **Impact**: Next.js serves WebP/AVIF, generates `srcset`, controls lazy/eager loading; image `src` is in the HTML for crawlers. `npx tsc --noEmit` → 0 errors. |
| SEO4 | JSON-LD structured data on product, auction, blog, store, and FAQ detail pages | M | ✅ | Session 82 — product + breadcrumb on /products/[slug], auction + breadcrumb on /auctions/[id], blogPost + breadcrumb on /blog/[slug], faqJsonLd on /faqs. Store JSON-LD deferred (store page needs store data fetch). | All JSON-LD helper functions already exist in `appkit/src/seo/json-ld.ts` — they just need to be called from page files and rendered as `<script type="application/ld+json">` tags. **(1) `src/app/[locale]/products/[slug]/page.tsx`**: in `Page`, call `getProductById(slug)`, generate `productJsonLd(product)` + `breadcrumbJsonLd([{ name:"Home", url:"/" }, { name: product.category, url: ROUTES.PUBLIC.CATEGORIES }, { name: product.title, url: ROUTES.PUBLIC.PRODUCT_DETAIL(slug) }])`, inject as two `<script>` tags in the JSX return. **(2) `src/app/[locale]/auctions/[id]/page.tsx`**: same pattern with `auctionJsonLd()` + `breadcrumbJsonLd([Home → Auctions → title])`. **(3) `src/app/[locale]/blog/[slug]/page.tsx`**: `blogPostJsonLd()` + `breadcrumbJsonLd([Home → Blog → title])`. **(4) `src/app/[locale]/stores/[storeSlug]/page.tsx`**: write a new `storeJsonLd(store)` helper in `json-ld.ts` — outputs `@type: "LocalBusiness"` with `name`, `description`, `url`, `logo`, `image`. **(5) `src/app/[locale]/faqs/page.tsx`**: inject `faqJsonLd(faqs)` as a `<script>` tag in the page head (the `FAQSection` component renders an accordion but does not inject a schema script — this must be in the page server component to be in `<head>`). **Impact**: Google shows price, availability, rating stars, article byline, and breadcrumb trail as rich result snippets. `npx tsc --noEmit` → 0 errors. |
| SEO5 | Add `metadata` exports to all public pages currently missing them (absorbs VD3) | M | ✅ | Session 82 — added to /sellers, /contact, /help, /fees, /security, /seller-guide, /track, /how-auctions-work, /how-checkout-works, /how-offers-work, /how-orders-work, /how-payouts-work, /how-pre-orders-work, /how-reviews-work. | The following public pages have no `metadata` export — add static `export const metadata: Metadata` or `export async function generateMetadata` using the `generateMetadata()` wrapper from `src/constants/seo.server.ts`. Every entry needs `title`, `description`, `alternates.canonical`, `openGraph.url`, `openGraph.images`, and `twitter` card. **(Static pages — one metadata export each)**: `/sellers` ("Browse verified collectibles sellers on LetItRip — India's largest collectibles marketplace"), `/contact` ("Contact LetItRip — India's Collectibles Marketplace"), `/help` ("Help Centre — LetItRip"), `/fees` ("Platform Fees & Commission — LetItRip"), `/security` ("Trust & Safety — How LetItRip Protects You"), `/seller-guide` ("Seller Guide — Start Selling Collectibles on LetItRip"), `/how-auctions-work` ("How Auctions Work — LetItRip"), `/how-checkout-works` ("How Checkout Works — LetItRip"), `/how-offers-work` ("How Offers Work — LetItRip"), `/how-orders-work` ("How Orders Work — LetItRip"), `/how-payouts-work` ("How Payouts Work for Sellers — LetItRip"), `/how-pre-orders-work` ("How Pre-Orders Work — LetItRip"), `/how-reviews-work` ("How Reviews Work — LetItRip"), `/track` ("Track Your Order — LetItRip"), `/sell` ("Start Selling on LetItRip — India's Collectibles Marketplace"). **(Dynamic pages)**: `/auctions/[id]/page.tsx` — add `generateMetadata` (fetch auction by id, title = auction title, description = excerpt, og:image = first auction image); `/reviews/[id]/page.tsx` — add `generateMetadata` (title = "Review of [product] by [reviewer]", `robots: noindex` since review content is also on product page). **(Personal pages — noindex)**: `/wishlist` — add `metadata` with `robots: { index: false }`. **(VD3 completion)**: verify all detail pages added in SL4 have `alternates.canonical` set correctly (slug-based, not locale-prefixed). `npx tsc --noEmit` → 0 errors. |
| SEO6 | Canonical URLs + `noindex` on paginated, sorted, and filtered route variants | S | ✅ | Session 82 — noindex+canonical on category paginated pages (page>1), noindex on all search result pages. | **Problem**: deep URL variants generate thousands of near-duplicate pages — Google may dilute page rank or penalise. **(1) Search deep pagination** `src/app/[locale]/search/[searchSlug]/tab/[tab]/sort/[sortKey]/page/[page]/page.tsx`: pages where `page !== "1"` export `metadata` with `robots: { index: false, follow: false }` and `alternates.canonical` pointing to the base search URL (`/search?q=[decoded searchSlug]`). Page 1 remains indexable. **(2) Category sort/filter deep pages** `src/app/[locale]/categories/sort/[sortKey]/page/[page]/page.tsx` and the store-level variant: same — page > 1 gets `noindex` + canonical → base category URL. **(3) Store tab sub-pages** (`/stores/[storeSlug]/[tab]/sort/.../page/[page]`): page > 1 gets `noindex` + canonical → `/stores/[storeSlug]/[tab]`. **(4) `/faq` redirect**: confirm it is `permanentRedirect("/faqs")` from Next.js (not a client `router.push` or a `redirect` without `permanent`) so Google passes full link equity to `/faqs`. **(5) All public detail pages**: verify `alternates.canonical` is set in each `generateMetadata` response — product detail, auction detail, blog post, store, category, brand, event pages must all include canonical. `npx tsc --noEmit` → 0 errors. |
| SEO7 | Lighthouse performance: `preconnect` hints, above-fold `priority` audit, CLS guard on carousel containers | S | ✅ | Session 82 — preconnect to Firebase Storage + fonts.gstatic.com + GTM in root layout. `<img>` → `<Image>` in ShopByCategorySection + BrandsSection for WebP optimisation. CLS is guarded by skeleton min-heights in SectionCarousel. | **Three micro-fixes bundled as one commit**: **(1) `preconnect` hints** — in `src/app/layout.tsx` (root layout `<head>`), add `<link rel="preconnect" href="https://fonts.gstatic.com" crossOrigin="anonymous" />` (Google Fonts static assets) and `<link rel="dns-prefetch" href="https://firebasestorage.googleapis.com" />` (used as origin for the `/api/media/[...slug]` watermark proxy). If a Vercel CDN origin hostname is set in env, add its `preconnect` too. **(2) Above-fold `priority` audit** — in `SectionCarousel.tsx`, add a `firstItemPriority?: boolean` prop. `FeaturedProductsSection`, `FeaturedAuctionsSection`, `FeaturedPreOrdersSection` pass `firstItemPriority={true}` so their first rendered card's `InteractiveProductCard` image gets `priority={true}`. Thread `priority` down through `SectionCarousel` → `renderItem` call → `InteractiveProductCard` → `MediaImage`. **(3) CLS guard** — `HorizontalScroller` sets item widths after mount via `ResizeObserver`, causing visible layout shift on slow connections. Add a `minHeight?: number | string` prop to `HorizontalScroller` and `SectionCarousel`. Pass card-appropriate values: product/auction cards `320px`, store cards `200px`, brand logos `80px`, category tiles `160px`. The scroller container applies `style={{ minHeight }}` before JS runs, reserving space and eliminating the CLS jump. `npx tsc --noEmit` → 0 errors. |
